$ #!/bin/bash

MAX_RETRIES=20
RETRY_DELAY=0.5

for ((i=1; i<=MAX_RETRIES; i++)); do
    echo "Attempt ${i} of ${MAX_RETRIES}"
    timeout 10 hostapd_cli status | grep "state=ENABLED"
    
    if [ $? -eq 0 ]; then
        echo "Command successful"
        exit 0
    else
        echo "Command failed, retrying in ${RETRY_DELAY} seconds..."
        sleep ${RETRY_DELAY}
    fi
done

echo "Failed to execute command after ${MAX_RETRIES} attempts"
exit 1


stdout:
Attempt 1 of 20
state=ENABLED
Command successful
